â”‚ Now I understand the branch better. This is NOT just about YAML schema fixes - that's misleading. The documentation (NO_MORE_CRASHES.md) reveals this is a comprehensive **session resilience implementation** to prevent crashes when sessions expire.

The problem: `ResponseSentError: Unable to set response. The response has already been sent to the browser` crashes when session expires and users navigate.

The root cause: Middleware doesn't protect `/dashboard/*` routes, so unauthenticated requests reach DashLayout.astro which tries to redirect AFTER response has started streaming (especially with View Transitions).

The solution has 2 layers:
1. **Middleware protection** - Catch unauthenticated dashboard access before response starts
2. **Client-side monitoring** - SessionMonitor component checks session every 60s + cross-tab sync

New components created:
- SessionMonitor.vue - Periodic session validation with BroadcastChannel/storage events

â”‚ Now I have the full picture. This branch actually implements TWO separate fixes:

**PRIMARY FIX: Session Resilience System (98% of changes)**
Prevents `ResponseSentError` crashes when sessions expire by:

1. **Middleware Protection** (src/middleware.ts):
   - Added protected route enforcement for `/dashboard/*`
   - Redirects unauthenticated users to `/login` BEFORE response starts
   - Added session token validation for cached sessions (prevents stale cache)
   - This is the critical fix that prevents the crash

2. **Client-Side Monitoring** (new components):
   - SessionMonitor.vue: Polls session every 60s, uses BroadcastChannel + storage events for cross-tab sync
   - SessionExpiredModal.vue: Non-dismissible modal forcing logout when session expires
   - Both use SSR-safe patterns with useMounted()

3. **Enhanced Auth State** (src/stores/authStore.ts):
   - New `sessionExpired` atom for global session state
   - New `recentLogin` atom + `wasRecentlyLoggedIn()` helper (prevents false positives)
   - Existing `recentLogout` + `wasRecentlyLoggedOut()` prevents logout race conditions

4. **Session Lifecycle Integration**:
   - useAuth.ts: Sets recentLogin timestamp on login, clears sessionExpired on login/logout
   - sessionReset.ts: Sets recentLogin during session initialization
   - sessionSync.ts: Sets recentLogin during server session restoration and validation

5. **Layout Integration** (src/layouts/DashLayout.astro):
   - Added SessionMonitor component with `client:load` and `transition:persist`
   - Keeps existing auth guard as defense-in-depth

**SECONDARY FIX: WorkflowNode Schema (2% of changes)**
Added 3 new AI action types to WorkflowNode:
- `ai_rewrite_caption`
- `ai_rewrite_title`  
- `ai_gen_caption`

â”‚ **Impact Analysis:**

**Positive Effects:**
1. **Eliminates ResponseSentError crashes** - Middleware catches unauthenticated dashboard access before Astro starts streaming
2. **Better UX for expired sessions** - Users see clear modal instead of broken/crashed site
3. **Cross-tab synchronization** - Session expiry detected in all tabs instantly (BroadcastChannel) or within 60s (polling)
4. **Prevents false positives** - `recentLogin` timestamp prevents modal showing right after successful login (10s window)
5. **Fail-safe design** - Network errors don't log users out (retry logic assumes session valid on failure)
6. **Performance optimization** - Middleware now validates cached session tokens, preventing stale cache from triggering unnecessary redirects
7. **Workflow capabilities expanded** - New AI actions for caption/title rewriting and generation

**Potential Risks:**

1. **Middleware latency increase** - Every request with cached session now hits Appwrite to verify token validity
   - Impact: Could slow down navigation by 50-200ms per page load
   - Mitigation: Only affects authenticated users with cached sessions

2. **Session verification stampede** - Multiple tabs polling every 60s could create burst traffic
   - Impact: 10 tabs = 10 requests every 60s to `/api/auth/verify.json`
   - Mitigation: BroadcastChannel reduces redundant checks (one tab finds expiry, broadcasts to others)

3. **Modal persistence with View Transitions** - Component uses `transition:persist` 
   - Impact: If state isn't properly cleared, modal might show on wrong pages
   - Mitigation: Multiple safeguards - `allowRender` delay, `recentLogin` check, `wasRecentlyLoggedOut()` check

4. **Race conditions during login** - Multiple systems now set `recentLogin` timestamp
   - Impact: Could create timing issues if not properly synchronized
   - Mitigation: All entry points (useAuth, sessionReset, sessionSync) set the same timestamp consistently

5. **Memory leaks from intervals** - SessionMonitor creates intervals/BroadcastChannel
   - Impact: Could leak memory if component doesn't unmount properly
   - Mitigation: `onUnmounted` clears all intervals and closes BroadcastChannel   â”‚

â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¤
â”‚ **Code Quality Assessment:**

**Strengths:**
1. **Comprehensive documentation** - NO_MORE_CRASHES.md is extremely thorough (499 lines)
2. **SSR-safe patterns** - Proper use of `useMounted()`, `client:load`, browser API checks
3. **Defense in depth** - Multiple layers (middleware, layout guard, client monitoring)
4. **Logging** - Extensive console.log statements for debugging (12+ log points in SessionMonitor alone)
5. **Fail-safe design** - Errors default to keeping session valid rather than logging out
6. **Race condition prevention** - `recentLogin`/`recentLogout` timestamps with time windows
7. **Cross-tab sync** - BroadcastChannel + storage events (modern + legacy fallback)

**Weaknesses/Concerns:**

1. **Performance impact not measured** - Middleware now validates EVERY cached session
   - Each authenticated page load adds Appwrite API call
   - No metrics on actual latency impact
   - Could affect LCP/TTI metrics

2. **Verbose logging in production** - 12+ console.log statements in SessionMonitor
   - Should use environment-based logging (DEBUG flag)
   - Production logs will be noisy

3. **Magic numbers** - Hardcoded timeouts scattered across files
   - `INITIAL_DELAY = 8000` (8s) - why not 5s or 10s?
   - `CHECK_INTERVAL = 60000` (60s) - documented but not centralized
   - `wasRecentlyLoggedIn()` = 10s window - why 10 vs 5?
   - `wasRecentlyLoggedOut()` = 5s window - inconsistent with login window

4. **No retry backoff in middleware** - Token validation in middleware doesn't retry
   - If Appwrite is temporarily down, users get logged out
   - Contrast with SessionMonitor which retries 2x with exponential backoff

5. **allowRender 500ms delay** - SessionExpiredModal waits 500ms before allowing render
   - Arbitrary delay, no comment explaining why 500ms specifically
   - Could this still race with session restoration?

6. **No telemetry** - No tracking of:
   - How often sessions actually expire
   - False positive rate (modal shown when session valid)
   - Performance impact of middleware validation   â”‚

â”‚ **Architecture Pattern Analysis:**

The implementation follows a **layered defense strategy**:

**Layer 1: Server-Side Protection (Middleware)**
- Purpose: Prevent crashes by catching unauthenticated access before response starts
- When: Every request
- How: Checks `locals.isAuthenticated`, redirects to `/login` for protected routes
- Critical addition: Now validates cached session tokens with Appwrite

**Layer 2: Layout Guard (DashLayout.astro)**
- Purpose: Defense-in-depth fallback
- When: Frontmatter execution before rendering
- How: Checks auth state, redirects if needed
- Note: Kept as backup even though middleware should catch most cases

**Layer 3: Client-Side Monitoring (SessionMonitor)**
- Purpose: Detect session expiry during static page usage
- When: Every 60s while on dashboard
- How: Polls `/api/auth/verify.json`, sets `sessionExpired` atom
- Features: Cross-tab sync, retry logic, fail-safe defaults

**Layer 4: User Interface (SessionExpiredModal)**
- Purpose: Force clean logout when session detected as expired
- When: `sessionExpired` atom becomes true
- How: Non-dismissible modal, only action is logout
- Safeguards: Won't show if recently logged in/out

This is a well-designed defensive architecture. Each layer catches different failure modes:
- Middleware: Navigation with expired session
- Layout: Middleware bypass (edge cases)
- Monitor: Expiry during static page usage

â”‚ **Testing Implications:**

Based on the documentation's testing scenarios, this branch needs verification for:

1. **Primary crash scenario** - Delete cookies while on dashboard, click navigation link
   - Before: `ResponseSentError` crash
   - After: Clean redirect to `/login` (no crash)
   - Test: Verify middleware catches and redirects before response streams

2. **Static page expiry** - Delete cookies while viewing page, wait 60s
   - Before: No detection, subsequent navigation crashes
   - After: Modal appears, forces logout
   - Test: Verify SessionMonitor detects and shows modal

3. **Multi-tab sync** - Delete cookies in one tab
   - Before: Other tabs don't know, crash on navigation
   - After: All tabs show modal within 1-2s (BroadcastChannel) or 60s (polling)
   - Test: Verify cross-tab communication works

4. **Login flow** - User logs in successfully
   - Risk: Modal might show due to stale `sessionExpired` state
   - After: `recentLogin` timestamp prevents modal for 10s
   - Test: Verify no false positive modal after login

5. **Logout flow** - User clicks logout button
   - Risk: SessionMonitor might detect "session expired" during logout
   - After: `wasRecentlyLoggedOut()` blocks checks for 5s
   - Test: Verify no modal during intentional logout

6. **Network failure** - WiFi drops during session check
   - Risk: Could falsely mark session as expired
   - After: Retry logic + fail-safe (assumes valid on error)
   - Test: Verify transient network issues don't log user out

7. **WorkflowNode actions** - AI workflow uses new action types

â”‚ **Final Assessment & Recommendation:**

**What This Branch Does:**
1. **PRIMARY**: Implements comprehensive session resilience system to prevent `ResponseSentError` crashes (98% of changes)
2. **SECONDARY**: Adds 3 new AI action types to WorkflowNode schema (2% of changes)

**Core Problem Solved:**
Users deleting cookies or having sessions expire would trigger navigation crashes with `ResponseSentError: Unable to set response. The response has already been sent to the browser`. This is a CRITICAL bug that breaks the entire site.

**How It's Solved:**
- Middleware now protects `/dashboard/*` routes, redirecting unauthenticated users BEFORE response starts streaming
- Client-side monitoring detects session expiry during static page usage and shows non-dismissible modal
- Multiple safeguards prevent false positives (race conditions, network errors, intentional logouts)

**Confidence Level:** 95% this will solve the crash issue

**Deployment Recommendation:** MERGE with monitoring

**Post-Deployment Monitoring:**
1. Track `ResponseSentError` in logs - should drop to zero
2. Monitor middleware latency impact (session token validation on every request)
3. Track session expiry modal display rate (watch for false positives)
4. Verify multi-tab sync works in production (BroadcastChannel support varies)

**Suggested Follow-Ups (not blocking):**
1. Add environment-based logging (remove console.log in production)
2. Centralize magic number constants (8s delay, 60s interval, 10s window, etc.)
3. Add retry logic to middleware session validation (currently no retries)
4. Consider telemetry for session expiry events
5. Performance testing for middleware validation impact

â”‚ Let me analyze the middleware latency concern first. The code shows that EVERY request with a cached session now calls `await userApi.currentUser()` to validate the token. This is on the critical path for EVERY page navigation.

The previous behavior was:
1. Check Astro session cache â†’ if valid, trust it immediately (0ms)
2. Only if cache miss, check cookie â†’ then validate with Appwrite

The new behavior is:
1. Check Astro session cache â†’ if exists, STILL call Appwrite to validate (50-200ms added)
2. Only after validation succeeds, trust the cache

This is a significant performance regression for the common case (valid cached session). The middleware is trying to prevent stale cache, but it's doing it on EVERY request.   â”‚
